window.addEventListener('load', function() {    
    function isIE() {
        const ua = window.navigator.userAgent;
        const msie = ua.indexOf('MSIE ');
        const trident = ua.indexOf('Trident/');
        
        return (msie > 0 || trident > 0);
    }
    
    function onLoad(){
        if(typeof window.WebPushManager !== "undefined"){
            window.WebPushManager(webPushConfiguration);
        }
    }
    
    if (isIE()) {
        return;
    }

    var webPushConfiguration = {
        serviceworker: '/sw.js',
        bundleSource: "https://cdn.dsmcdn.com/mweb/production/client.7f1de7a56ca9e5783eaa.bundle.js",
        publicKey: "BG_jWaqkfRYx9z0eoQeMqinCCQk2ZNPb1ibUKqgMc2ROzTflwckrFQPBzR7wca_xiThRtvIcDJj1EUnEzTcOYlU",
        subscriptionHost: "https://apigw.trendyol.com/discovery-storefrontmarketing-webpushcollector-service",
        platformId: "1",
        storefrontId: "1",
    };

    var script = document.createElement('script');
    script.defer = true;
    script.src = webPushConfiguration.bundleSource;
    script.onload = onLoad;

    document.body.appendChild(script);
});


    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
        sendAbTestingPageViewEvent();
    });

    function sendAbTestingPageViewEvent() {
        if (window.hasOwnProperty('_gcol')) {
            const now = new Date().getTime().toString();
    
            const Ab = getCookieValue("AbTesting") || '';
            const msearchAb = getCookieValue("msearchAb") || '';
            const recoAb = getCookieValue("recoAb") || '';
            const janusAbTestCookieValue = Ab.split("|")[0];

            const abTestingCookieValue = [msearchAb, recoAb, janusAbTestCookieValue].filter(Boolean).join('-');
    
            if (!abTestingCookieValue) {
                return;
            }

            const eventData = {
                ts: now,
                channel: 'web',
                event: 'ty_analytics',
                tv007: '0',
                tv019: window.location.href,
                tv020: window.TYPageName || window.page_type || window.pageType,
                tv037: now,
                tv066: window.navigator.userAgent,
                tv230: 'WEBABTEST',
                tv231: 'ty_assignmentapi',
                tv232: janusAbTestCookieValue
            };
            
            window._gcol.Fire("ty_analytics", eventData);
        }
    }

}

function OptanonWrapper() {

        });

    }

        var oneTrustBFCacheIgnoreHandler = () => {
          try {
            const isClosed = _gcol.ReadCookie("OptanonAlertBoxClosed");
            if (isClosed) {
              OneTrust.Close();
              OneTrust.AllowAll();
              removeEventListener("pageshow", oneTrustBFCacheIgnoreHandler);
            }
          } catch (e) {
            console.error(e.message);
            removeEventListener("pageshow", oneTrustBFCacheIgnoreHandler);
          }
        };
        addEventListener("pageshow", oneTrustBFCacheIgnoreHandler);
      }
    }

    OneTrust.OnConsentChanged(function (event) {

        clearCookies();

    });

  }

  demeterScript.defer = true;
  demeterScript.src = "https://cdn.dsmcdn.com/sfint/production/demeter-prod-1-1-0.umd.js";
  
  const config = {
    baseUrl: "https://demeter-tr-core-collect.trendyol.com",
    logLevel: "none",
    environment: "production",
    namespace: "tr-ecommerce",
    commonData: {
      overrides: {

      }
    },
    delphoiConfig: {
      isAdaptEnabled: "true" === "true",
      delphoiScreenToDemeterScreenMap: pageTypes,
      delphoiEventsToDemeterEventGroupsMap: eventsMap
    }
  };

  demeterScript.onload = async () => {
    const demeterInstance = new window.Demeter({ config });
    try {
      await demeterInstance.init();
      window.dispatchEvent(new Event("demeterReady"));
    } catch (e) {
      console.log(e);
    }
  };
